  <script>
    (function () {
      if (window.PerformanceObserver) {
        window._perfMarkAllowedList = [
        'cx-candybar-onload',
        'first-contentful-paint',
        'cx-candybar-onload',
        'gcRendererStart',
        'gpt-tagLoaded',
        'gpt-slotRequested',
        'gpt-slotRenderEnded',
        'gpt-slotOnload',
        'optimizely:blockBegin',
        'playerLoadStart',
        'playerReady',
        'playerDisplayed',
        'prebidAuctionInit',
        'prebidAuctionEnd',
        'reactAppRenderStart',
        'reactAppRenderEnd',
        'apstag-loaded',
        'apstag-firstBid',
        'moat-loaded',
        'moat-ace-firstAdItem',
        'moat-uac-firstAdItem',
        'djcmp-loaded',
        'djcmp-vendor-loaded',
        'djcmp-tcdata-loaded'
      ];
        var observer = new PerformanceObserver(function (list) {
          var entries = list.getEntries();
          var _loop = function _loop(i) {
            var entry = entries[i];
            var metricName = entry.name;
            if ( window._perfMarkAllowedList.indexOf(entry.name) !== -1 ) {
              var time = Math.round(entry.startTime + entry.duration);
              if (metricName === 'gpt-slotOnload' ) {
                if (typeof newrelic !== 'undefined') {
                  newrelic.setCustomAttribute(metricName, time);
                }
                setTimeout(function(){observer.disconnect()}, 8000)
              } else {
                if (typeof newrelic !== 'undefined') {
                  newrelic.setCustomAttribute(metricName, time);
                }
              }
            }
          };
          for (var i = 0; i < entries.length; i++) {
            _loop(i);
          }
        });
        try {
          observer.observe({
            type: ['mark'], buffered: true
          });
        }
        catch(e) {
          console.log('observer not supported')
        }
      }
    })();
    //INP code below
    (()=> {
    var highestInp = 0;
    var observer = new PerformanceObserver((list, obs, options) => {
      for (var entry of list.getEntries()) {
        if (!entry.interactionId) continue;
        var duration = Math.round(entry.duration);
        if (duration <= highestInp) continue;
        highestInp = duration;
        var startTime = Math.round(entry.startTime);

        var label = entry.target && entry.target.ariaLabel ? entry.target.ariaLabel.replaceAll(" ", "_") : undefined;
        label = label ? label : (entry.target ? entry.target.localName : undefined);
        var selector = entry.target && entry.target.classList && entry.target.classList.value ? entry.target.classList.value.replaceAll(" ", "_") : undefined;
        if (!selector) {
          selector = entry.target && entry.target.parentElement && entry.target.parentElement.ariaLabel ? entry.target.parentElement.ariaLabel.replaceAll(" ", "_") : 
            (entry.target && entry.target.parentElement ? entry.target.parentElement.localName : undefined);
        }
        if (!label || !selector) {
          // likely video
          label = label ? label : (window.utag_data ? window.utag_data.user_type : undefined);
          var hasVideo = document.querySelector('[data-type="video"]')
          selector = selector ? selector : hasVideo ? 'video' : 'no-video';
        }
        var target = label + ':' + selector;
        if (window.newrelic) {
          if (window.requestIdleCallback) {
            requestIdleCallback(() => {
              newrelic.setCustomAttribute('inpSlowEventTarget', target);
              newrelic.setCustomAttribute('inpSlowEventStartTime', startTime);
            });
          } else {
            newrelic.setCustomAttribute('inpSlowEventTarget', target);
            newrelic.setCustomAttribute('inpSlowEventStartTime', startTime);
          }
        }
      }
    });
    try {
      observer.observe({
        type: 'event',
        durationThreshold: 200, // good INP is under 200ms
        buffered: true
      });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('PerformanceObserver failed', error)
    }
  })();

  </script>

        <header class="header header--secondary">
            <h2 class="title">
                <span class="label">Ford Motor Co.</span>
            </h2>
        </header>

            <p class="description__text">Ford Motor Co. engages in the manufacture, distribution, and sale of automobiles. It operates through the following segments: Ford Blue, Ford Model E, and Ford Pro, Ford Next, and Ford Credit. The Ford Blue, Ford Model E, and Ford Pro segment includes the sale of Ford and Lincoln vehicles, service parts, and accessories, together with the associated costs to develop, manufacture, distribute, and service the vehicles, parts, and accessories. The Ford Next segment focuses on development costs for autonomous vehicles and related businesses, equity ownership in Argo AI, and other mobility businesses and investments. The Ford Credit segment is involved in the credit business on a consolidated basis, which is primarily vehicle-related financing and leasing activities. The company was founded by Henry Ford on June 16, 1903 and is headquartered in Dearborn, MI.</p>
